NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE
PUBLIC NOTICE
G. Rajendran, the Managing Trustee, GRT Mahalakshmi Educational Charitable Trust (Formerly known as Sola Raju
Dhanuskodi Raja Thai Ammal Memorial Educational Charitable Trust, formed on 30th of November 2001 and registered
with the office of the Sub-Registrar Office-II, Saidapet, Chennai, Tamil Nadu vide Document No. 445 of 2001) here notify
the following:—
The name of the Sola Raju Dhanuskodi Raja Thai Ammal Memorial Educational Charitable Trust has been
changed as GRT Mahalakshmi Educational Charitable Trust with effect from May 2011 vide Document No. 365 of 2011
registered with office of the Sub-Registrar Office-II, Saidapet, Chennai, Tamil Nadu.
For GRT MAHALAKSHMI EDUCATIONAL CHARITABLE TRUST
Chennai-600 017,
9th June 2011.
